    FROM [Artists] AS [a]

) AS [t]
LEFT JOIN [Artworks] AS [a0] ON [t].[id] = [a0].[ArtistId]
LEFT JOIN [Galleries] AS [g] ON [t].[id] = [g].[InitiatorId]
ORDER BY [t].[id], [a0].[id]
